          <div class=" ddc-content content-default" data-widget-id="content1" data-widget-name="content-default">
           <h3 class="h1 ddc-heading-1 widget-heading">
            Welcome to Jeff Wyler Eastgate Auto Mall
           </h3>
           <div class="content">
            <b>
             <font size="3">
              Jeff Wyler Eastgate Auto Mall
             </font>
            </b>
            <br/>
            Jeff Wyler Eastgate Auto Mall is proud to be your premier Cincinnati new &amp; used car dealership, located minutes from downtown at the Eastgate Auto Mall. We feature multiple new car dealerships at one location, including Chevrolet, Chrysler, Jeep, Dodge, RAM, Mazda, Nissan and Kia, as well as our huge used car dealership. Take some time to search our large inventory of
            <a href="/new-inventory/index.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="new cars for sale in Cincinnati">
             new cars for sale in Cincinnati
            </a>
            , and if you don't find the car, truck, SUV or van you desire - no worries! Jeff Wyler has multiple dealerships in Ohio, Kentucky, and Indiana to choose from, we will move the new or used car you want to Jeff Wyler Eastgate Auto Mall.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <font size="3">
             <b>
              Auto Repair &amp; Service in Batavia
             </b>
            </font>
            <br/>
            Our friendly auto repair departments features modern service bays and diagnostic equipment to expertly handle your vehicle's scheduled maintenance, as well as handling common fixes like brake repair, transmission repair, new tires and alignment, oil changes, tune-ups, batteries, and more. You can schedule your
            <a href="/schedule-service.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="service appointment online">
             service appointment online
            </a>
            at your convenience. If you need genuine OEM
            <a href="/parts/index.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="car parts and accessories in Batavia">
             car parts and accessories in Batavia
            </a>
            , our parts department can provide or locate what you need.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <font size="3">
             <b>
              Your Ohio New &amp; Used Car Dealership
             </b>
            </font>
            <br/>
            Our Jeff Wyler Eastgate Auto Mall dealership is located at
            <a href="/dealership/directions.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="1117 State Route 32, Batavia, OH 45103">
             1117 State Route 32, Batavia, OH 45103
            </a>
            , on the east side of Cincinnati. As one of the highest rated car dealers in Ohio, our customers come from throughout the tristate, including northern KY and Indiana. Some of the areas our customers come from include Cincinnati, Loveland, Goshen, Mount Repose, Milford, Summerside, Amelia, Williamsburg, Mount Orab, Hillsboro, Georgetown, Bethel, New Richmond, New Hope, and Beechmont.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <font size="3">
             <b>
              Auto Insurance
             </b>
            </font>
            <br/>
            <a href="https://agents.allstate.com/william-bristow-batavia-oh.html" internallink="false" target="_self" title="undefined">
             <img class="wysiwyg-image" href="//pictures.dealer.com/j/jeffwylereastgateautomall/0608/15665a82cc417d1be2cb739d38953b9fx.jpg" src="//pictures.dealer.com/j/jeffwylereastgateautomall/0608/15665a82cc417d1be2cb739d38953b9fx.jpg" style="border-width: 0px;" tabindex="30000" title="Allstate.PNG"/>
            </a>
            <br/>
            Jeff Wyler Eastgate Auto Mall is proud to announce the addition of a new Allstate Insurance Agency to the suite of services we provide our customers. Conveniently located at our Jeff Wyler Eastgate Auto Mall dealership in our Kia building. We provide auto insurance, motorcycle insurance, home insurance, renters insurance, flood insurance, business insurance, life insurance and other Allstate Insurance products to meet all your insurance needs. You can get an insurance quote by simply stopping by, when you are purchasing your new car or while you're car in being serviced. Please visit our site,
            <a href="https://agents.allstate.com/william-bristow-batavia-oh.html" internallink="false" target="_self" title="Wyler Insurance Services">
             Wyler Insurance Services
            </a>
            , to get more information on the Allstate products and services we have to offer.
